In[32]:
# read all Stokes files
lbl = 'AGPJV'

fi = np.sort(glob(dirc+'*I_'+lbl+'*fits'))
fq = np.sort(glob(dirc+'*Q_'+lbl+'*fits'))
fu = np.sort(glob(dirc+'*U_'+lbl+'*fits'))
fv = np.sort(glob(dirc+'*V_'+lbl+'*fits'))

ff = [fi,fq,fu,fv] # store in a list
In[36]:
#---
# read all fits files and make a 4D array [ns, ny, nw, nx] 
#---
dat = fits.open(fi[0])[1].data.squeeze()
nw, ny = dat.shape

stks = np.zeros((4, len(fi), nw, ny))  # make empty array
      
hdrinfo = []
tims = []

for k in tqdm(range(0,4)):
    for j in range(len(fi)):
        
        hdr  = fits.open(ff[k][j])[1].header
        dat = fits.open(ff[k][j])[1].data   #for Na D1 I
        #stks[j,cc,:,:] = dat[:,:].squeeze()
        #hdrinfo.append(hdr)
        tims.append(hdr['Date-Avg'])
        stks[k,j,:,:] = dat[:,:].squeeze()

ns, ny, nw, nx = stks.shape

# now see the stokes profiles

ax = ax.flatten()

lbls = ['Stokes I/I$_c$', 'Stokes Q/I$_c$', 'Stokes U/I$_c$','Stokes V/I$_c$' ]
for i in range(4):
    mm = np.mean(stks[:,10:20,:,10:20], axis=(1,3))  # mean of QS pixels
    ax[i].plot(wav, mm[i,:])
    ax[i].set_title(lbls[i])
    ax[i].set_xlim(wav[455],wav[660])  # wavelength limit to see Fe I 6301 line pair
plt.tight_layout()
